368:

Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
Is the formation date of the association football club whose official website is http://www.chievoverona.it/ (this statement is in the Italian language) in the year 1946?

### SPARQL:
SELECT
WHERE
  {
    ?club a :;
           :formationDate ?formationDate.

    ?formation :formationDate ?formationDate.
    FILTER (?formationDate = 1)
  }

634:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
Of the films in the Shrek franchise of animated features—which has an official website of http://www.shrek.com—which one made the most at the box office?

### SPARQL:
SELECT
  ?film
  ?film_box_office
  ?film_title
  ?film
WHERE
  ?film a ?film_type
  ?film_type rdfs:label ?film_type_label
  ?film
  ?film_box_office rdfs:label ?film_box_office_label
  ?film_box_office rdfs:value ?film_box_office_value
  ?film_title
  ?film_title rdf
  FILTER

  (?film_box ?film_box_office_label)
  (?film_box_office ?film)
  (?film_title ?film_title_label)
  (?film ?film_type_label)
  (?film_type)
  (?film_box_office_value ?film_box_office_value)
  (?film_box_office ?film_box_office_label)
  (?film_title_label ?film)
  (?film_type ?film

999:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What is the Instagram username for the national-association football team whose ranking is equal to 12 (the point in time of this statement is 2007-12-17)?

### SPARQL:
SELECT ?
WHERE
  ?foo a :National Football Team.
  ?foo : ?foo.
  ?foo :ranking ?rank.
  FILTER (?rankcury = 12)

##
###
### IN

### INSP
SELECT ?foo

###
### INSPARQL
SELECT ?foo
WHERE
  ?foo a : :National Football Team.
  ?foo :foo ?foo.
  ?foo :foo ?foo.
  ?foo :foo :rank ?rankcury.
  FILER (?rankcury = 12)

### INSPAR
SELECT ?foo
WHERE
  ?foo a :National Football Team.
  ?foo :foo ?foo.
  ?foo :foo ?foo.
  ?foo :ranking ?rankcury.
  FILTER (?rankcury = 1)

### IN
SELECT ?foo
WHERE
  ?foo a :National Football Team.
